name:Kâ€aâ€zâ€zâ€yâ€ â€tâ€râ€aâ€vâ€eâ€lâ€eâ€r
info:Deluxe Queen Room
info:Stayed in June 2023
info:Business travelers
info:4 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted July 17, 2023
msg:Zhonglian GDH Hotel - finally back after  4 years.  8 nights in room 1718 "Deluxe Queen", at the back.  Reasonably quiet this time, probably due to the lack of traffic and fewer guests - meaning less banging doors. Very dark. Bed was actually a king size and wasn't too firm. I slept well most nights. International power points with USB ports. Adjustable and very cold aircon had no trouble in the 36C heat. Good water pressure with rain and hand showers.  No bath.  Some marks on the carpet and chair upholstery. Good buffet breakfast with eggs to order. Chinese bacon.  Baked beans some mornings.  Lots of sweet options and pastries and several types of fresh fruits such as watermelon, dragonfruit and pineapple. Automatic coffee machine coffee that was almost drinkable on a couple of mornings but mostly bad. I really enjoyed the room service shrimp fried rice on several nights and there is a new McDonald's and KFC close by.  Almost no english tv channels.  No smart tv. 

I have stayed here many times over the last decade but this time the GDH was very quiet with me being the only westerner that I saw in the hotel on most days. Not sure if the new Marriott has caused this.

Lovely help from the customer service managers- even helping me order online food since I don't read Chinese and everything is now done by an app.

Limited internet access in Jiangsu that blocked my Gmail, even though I could download it in Zhejiang.  One day my webmail was also totally blocked but mysteriously became accessible again the next.
